This screams synthetic air.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2317730"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2317730#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2315633" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2246319">purebrainrot</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-07">10/07/24 22:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The initial spray gives you the faint, sweet smell of pears and green apples. The dry down goes quickly into musk and powder. It reminds me of a quiet library or lobby area on a cloudy, cold fall morning. It gives off a mature, clean vibe that can make someone feel productive and put together. <br />
It isn't too elegant and can be worn for everyday wear, and it's a perfect base to layer other scents with. I would definitely add this to my rotation if I could afford it. The high price point is unfortunately the greatest drawback for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2308436"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2308436#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2307787" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1947453">Fragrance_Nolan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-05">10/05/24 11:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>At the store I thought Another 13 smelled pretty amazing, fruity floral powdery a little woodiness and musk. Beautiful-smelling without being citrus-focused and not heavy nor punchy, it's everything I'm looking for in a light fragrance for the cooler weather. Unfortunately testing a new bottle at home, there's not much to the scent it just smells like hot candle wax to me maybe it's the musk but there's not much else to the scent profile. I'm guessing the formula has to sit and mature for the ingredients to open up, which is what I'm planning on doing. It reminds me a bit of Chanel fragrances but not as elegant, maybe it's the way the musk is used in both. I'm also not getting the funky smell that a lot of people talk about. I think Another 13 is a good fragrance for someone who doesn't want to wear fragrances but has to or dislikes more complex scent profiles and wants something simplistic. With the scent I experienced at the perfume store, I'd give Le Labo's Another 13 a 9/10, excellent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2305890"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2305890#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2302796" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Magazine paper, as many have said, is definitely right. Completely safe for work, but not many will be able to tell if that pleasant smell is coming from you or the freshly cleaned low pile office carpet. Contrary to a lot of reviews, I found Another 13 to lean very masculine from start to finish. My head-canon is that this is the default factory scent that sexy android Connor from 'Detroit Become Human' comes with.<br />
<br />
Only sprayed twice and longevity was insane- took over 24 hours to fade, even withstanding a halfhearted scrub.<br />
<br />
Edit: I showered, scrubbed, exfoliated with a loofah 4 hours ago and I still smell Another 13 with my wrist just a few inches from my face. Wear this if you want it to just be how your whole life smells from now on.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2235919"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2235919#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2230563" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2213181" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="rrrouge"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1023834"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1023834.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="rrrouge" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Comme-des-Garcons/Zero-74318.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.74318.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Zero"title="Zero"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2213181ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2213181" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1023834">rrrouge</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-09">07/09/24 12:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Unreal. Deceptively simple. A work of art. This scent is chic, cerebral, intimate, potent, and emotionally stirring all at once. I read a review that described this as "simultaneously cold and warm, sharp and soft [...] It smells like metal and also like a baby's head. It's kind of heartbreaking".<br />
<br />
This stands out from other gorgeous musky scents to me (like PDM Valaya) because it's obviously synthetic but with a warm, skin-like quality that feels like an all-encompassing embrace from a loved one. <br />
<br />
Aside from its emotional impact, I love its elusive quality and incredible scent trail. Sometimes it feels like I'm wearing nothing then I'll get hypnotic wafts that make me stop in my tracks and breathe deeply, or a stranger will chase me down the train station to ask what I'm wearing. If this performs weakly for you, you might be anosmic to some or all of its notes.<br />
<br />
You'll need time to appreciate all its nuances. It's an experience. Movement and heat makes it come alive. Wear it while running errands. Spray it on a scarf in the summer or leave a sample in a bag you don't usually use. It'll enthrall you when you come back to it months later.<br />
<br />
This is what made me fall in love with perfumery and olfactory memory.<br />
<br />
A scent for that mysterious person who's here one moment and gone the next, but when they're around they're intoxicating.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2213181"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2213181#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2212508" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I’ve always been curious about Le Labo because of the lore and the hype and the branding. It became immediately clear upon first sniff, this brand does not work with my chemistry. The same thing happened with Dedcool- I wanted to like it, and I could see vision, but damn UGH that and this shit smell gross to me.<br />
<br />
The first sniff, just out of the package not on my skin yet, it smells exactly like magazines, the glossy paper, the ink, the faint vague perfume sample smell. Which could be nostalgic and cute but I’m sensitive to fragrance and it immediately felt like a future migraine. And very plasticky in a way, not warm or sweet.<br />
<br />
I did dab, not spray, a bit on my wrist, because I wanted to give it a chance in my skin. Honestly<br />
I disliked it the whole time. I felt it change and develop- it did age and gain more warmth and distance- losing the first stark alcoholic intensity- but it still felt so artificial. I felt like I was trapped in a mall. Which is hellish to me. High key, I definitely have fragrance allergies which ruins my experiences of a lot of perfumes. But occasionally I give them a chance, sometimes I find ones that work. <br />
<br />
For now, I had to thoroughly wash my wrists, then reapplied cocoa butter and my favorite orange vetiver essential oils. I think I’ll just stick to my basics.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2204460"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2204460#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2203766" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I sprayed it on my skin yesterday and - absolutely nothing. Not a hint of anything. I'm guessing I'm completely anosmic to the Iso E Super in this. Disappointed, I went on with my day. After a few hours, a noticed a weirdly artificial smell lingering around me - clean, warm and icy cold at the same time. I sniffed my arm and it was bloody Another 13 remembering its own existence, apparently, because now I could finally smell it. A robotic, hardly human, business airport lounge smell. I'll be sure to test this one out again and update my review, but so far - in love with the way this smells... almost a full day after spraying it.<br />
<br />
Edit : got a 30ml of this the day after writing this "review" because I hate financial stability but love smelling like a half-human android wrapped in a cozy blanket giving out free hugs. This time, I'm able to smell it as soon as I spray it - and it's divinely weird. Amazing !</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2203766"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2203766#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2203405" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2203405" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="chamberlain"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2156453"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2156453.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="chamberlain" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2203405ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2203405" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2156453">chamberlain</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-29">06/29/24 18:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>What a scent! The opening of Another 13 is light and airy, with a subtle sweetness that gently unfolds. The ambroxan provides a clean, almost skin-like scent. It's a fragrance that sits close to the skin for the wearer and one that is projected for an observer. The sillage is moderate, making it perfect for both office wear and casual outings. It’s a fragrance that invites people closer, rather than announcing your presence from across the room.<br />
<br />
It's important to note that overspraying can bring out an undesirable alcohol smell, the strength of which is especially dependent on the batch that you have. The dry down remains the same regardless.<br />
<br />
Another fascinating aspect of Another 13 is its ability to become almost imperceptible to the wearer after some time. This phenomenon, often referred to as "nose fatigue," can make it seem like the fragrance has faded away. However, don't be fooled—this scent can creep up on you and others around you throughout the day. You'll catch unexpected whiffs of its subtle, captivating aroma, reminding you of its enduring presence.<br />
<br />
Truly a 10/10 fragrance for me</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2203405"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2203405#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2202085" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I don't like them, and they don't like me. But over the past year I've come a long way in expanding my... nose palate...? in the perfume world, and it has paid off with other genres. I figured I'd go after the most applauded musk scents to tempt my schnoz into enjoying musks, starting strong with Another 13 and Glossier You.<br />
<br />
Unfortunately, this did what musky/ISO E scents always do on me. It smelled strongly, sharply, of a big ol' man's BO. Not just sweat, my friends, but the kind of stale and over the top stank that makes one wonder how to gently tell a friend that they really should shower more often.<br />
<br />
Look, I'm not trying to knock it. This is a personal beef that I have with musk and musk has with me. It smelled okay on my guy friend; his wife actually complained because she loved the smell on him so much and they can't afford to buy it. But within minutes, on me, it is not a scent, but a stench. This was confirmed by the very same friend on whom it was just fine. The frontal-lobe-piercing odour that is so offensively strong on me doesn't, obviously, happen to everyone, and on other people, I find it perfectly acceptable. On me, uh, not so much.<br />
<br />
I don't think my Glossier sample is gonna go significantly better, is it?<br />
<br />
Jeez, musk, I never did anything bad to you, there's absolutely zero need to do me like this...<br />
<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1565630">lapharme</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-23">06/23/24 17:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>So I just tried my sample of this again after trying it earlier this year in much colder weather and hardly smelling anything at all. Wow! NOW I get it! This baby apparently just needs heat for me, because in the winter it smelled like nothing but pure iso-e-super which to me basically smells like almost nothing. But NOW I’m smelling all those other notes! Fig, musk, ambrette, ambroxan, something creamy that is kind of like vanilla-almond, but yet, it isn’t (edit: I think it’s sandalwood! A very milky, sweet, slightly cedar-y sandalwood). That’s just right off the top of my head! It’s almost like a SUPER light, airy, true summertime version of Hypnotic Poison, like a summertime l’eau edc or something! I LOVE it!!!! It’s so weird, it doesn’t actually smell LIKE Hypnotic Poison, but to me it truly smells like what a perfect TRUE HOT WEATHER interpretation of it would smell like! It’s got that creamy, cozy, almondy depth that HP has, but is otherwise entirely fresh, clean, airy, and light. I’m actually recovering from a really nasty case of food poisoning right now and I can’t really stand to wear any perfumes, but at the same time I really wanted to wear one (just knew 99.9% would make me sicker in my current state and might ruin the perfume for me) but this one was so different in that regard and I figured if anything I just wouldn’t smell it at all like last time. Well I did smell it this time! But it’s still uniquely fresh light and airy enough to not be bothersome at all in my current condition, which is amazing! Hell, for that reason alone I may need a bottle, this would be my “palate cleanser” of sorts, and also a great soothing option from when recovering from illness or even just anytime I’m feeling a bit queasy, this is one of those extremely rare perfumes that not only is not bothersome in such a state but is actually helpful, it actually seems to calm and center me and pushes the other unpleasant smells of the world that may make me more nauseous out. I’m definitely strongly considering a bottle now and probably will buy one. While I love my big, bold, dramatic scents, sometimes what enchants me more than anything is such a clean, therapeutic, almost air-like fresh scent as this! There are tons of freshies out there, but that doesn’t mean there aren’t still masterpieces hidden among them! A good fresh scent can be every single bit as masterful as a deep scent on the opposite end of the spectrum, they seem perhaps even harder to achieve (especially with good performance too)! Now that I’ve got to experience this perfume properly, I can honestly say that I have yet to have a single miss from Le Labo.<br />
<br />
If you like perfumes such as:<br />
MFK BR540<br />
Jo Malone Wood Sage &amp; Sea Salt<br />
Hermes Eau de Merveilles and the other fresh “Merveilles” ie bleu, clair<br />
Creed silver mountain water <br />
Escentric molecules molecule 01<br />
JHAG not a perfume <br />
<br />
<br />
You should definitely give this one a try too!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2197533"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2197533#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2193634" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; You know when people here claim a fragrance to be a "love at first sniff"? I would think, "What a silly thing to say". Well, I guess I'm the silliest person on the planet because that's exactly what happened to me when I first sampled Another 13. It's crisp and floral but also mineral. There is something inhuman about it too, which makes it all the more alluring. I bought the 50ml about 8 months ago, and I think I'm about 1-2 months away from finishing it (I have never finished a bottle of anything in my life!). I crave this thing— all the time. I've tried to find other scents and use other fragrances that I've owned for years, but I can't stay away from A13 for too long. This scent has also been the first to get me multiple compliments from family, friends, and complete strangers. So strange.<br />
<br />
<br />
UPD. I gave it another go, sprayed a bit more this time and I can smell it this time around. And you guys, I love it. It was one of those days I was not feeling wearing like any perfume so I thought something light would do it. And it is so clean and refreshing, but without any citrus in it. It’s very unique. Sweet on my skin. But gets saltier with time. Incredible. I don’t have anything to compare it with. Kinda like baby powder but in a good way. With some subtle pickles from Santal 33 whispering far in the distance. Leaning feminine on me. Ultimate clean girl fragrance. But not so girly like Not a Perfume. I can see it being masculine leaning on a man. Hell yeah I want my partner to smell like this regardless of their gender. It’s very complex in a very subtle way. It’s giving “your skin but better”. One more LE LABO I’m in love with.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2179833"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2179833#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2177936" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2177936" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ien4444"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2015811"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2015811.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ien4444" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Fueguia-1833/Yaguarete-Edition-2016-67040.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.67040.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Yaguarete Edition 2016"title="Yaguarete Edition 2016"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2177936ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2177936" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2015811">ien4444</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-04">06/04/24 12:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Every time I smell this perfume I have a different experience. It phases between a soft powdery clean girl, saran wrap cling film, yuzu-flavored seltzer water, hotel lobby (the kind that boasts Aesop soaps), and a celluloid iso-e reminiscent of that sterile hay in Żubrówka. At the same time, it's a sternly linear scent... As my coworker says, maybe it's not the scent that changes but it's you that's different. <br />
<br />
I bought two samples twice before committing to the 100mL. It's the perfect formula to “smell nice” in an abstract way. Layering with other fragrances brings a sunny daytime clarity to even the sluttiest of musks. No matter how much I use, it never becomes cloying... wearing this is like multiplying by zero. I found myself reaching for samples after work while still in the city-- especially on the subway when someone else's odor was unbearable. It didn't seem to offend or overwhelm anyone nearby despite us being in an enclosed space. It's the perfect intensity and pleasantness for a client meeting, too. <br />
<br />
Another 13 is the Q Tonic of the fragrance world. Or perhaps The Row's version of a simple leather tote. You don't buy it because people notice; you buy it because you're detail-oriented and have money to stave-off your ennui with all things ordinary. In this case, one's skin scent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2177936"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2177936#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2177848" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2074474">Ajlis</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-04">06/04/24 10:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Another 13 makes me feel clean — not in a shower-fresh kind of way, but clean like cool wind or freshly washed clothes that have just come out of the dryer. It’s an airy, slightly woody scent with a hint of metal and fresh pear in the opening – light yet musky at the same time. At the heart of the scent are notes of ambroxan and Iso E Super, which I recognize from other "my skin but better" type perfumes. However, my absolute favorite among the skin scents is Diptyque's L'eau Papier, which is softer and more natural, and has lovely notes of rice and sesame. Another 13 is similar but more synthethic. Owning a bottle of L'eau Papier, I don't need Another 13 in my collection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2177848"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2177848#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2176967" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1565630">lapharme</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-03">06/03/24 11:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Yeah this ain’t it, and I got the manufacturer’s sample so I doubt it’s fake. This is just iso-e-super, the other notes are barely detectable. I can only half-smell it, a feat characteristic of iso-e, and I don’t like that. I want to be able to smell my perfume, that’s kind of the whole point to me. It’s just very boring, out of all the aromachemicals, I’m just not a big fan of iso-e, and I like others a lot. So that’s a personal preference issue I guess, but my other gripe with this is that there really isn’t much else to it at all. Hardly anything. The other notes are seriously BARELY there. They might as well not be. This is basically like pure iso-e super, like the escentric molecules one or literally just pure iso-e super diluted in alcohol which is what that perfume is anyway. And it’s a LOT cheaper. Therefore, this is kind of a ripoff. I CANNOT believe all the hype!! This is one of the ONLY fragrances I’ve ever had heavily hyped up to me in real life, and not just on the internet. I don’t usually talk to people about perfume irl so that’s huge. And my god what a let down! I love other Le Labo scents too, I have Santal 33 and it’s one of my favorite and most worn perfumes this spring, and I also love Rose 31 and Tonka 25 and plan on buying as well as the dc’d Vanille 44 which is an elusive holy grail type of perfume for me, but Another 13 ain’t it at all. The performance also really sucked, very much UNLIKE the other Le Labos I’ve tried. Definitely don’t blind buy this, not because it’s offensive, but because it’s just a waste of money imo and chances are, you’ll be disappointed. It’s just not much of anything at all. And I love scents like BR540 and Glossier You so I was thinking this would be along the lines of those, but it’s not, not at all. It’s not “transparent” or “skin-like”, it’s just bland and empty. I’m SO glad I didn’t blind buy this like I was considering!!!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2176801"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2176801#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2175883" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I received a lot of compliments from those around me, especially when I layered it with "Cacharel-Noa". It is a clean scent that will make you smell like a "Clean-Girly" but this comment is definitely made according to my nose.Since there are many molecules in its notes, it may vary from nose to nose. <br />
<br />
It definitely needs to be given a chance, because if your nose is not used to molecular perfumes, you may not like it very much at first, but you can get used to it over time.<br />
<br />
I don't think men need to layer this perfume, but if you want to layer it, it would be good for you to layer it with musk-based perfumes.<br />
<br />

I avoid extremely feminine fragrances when I work in the field, my objective is to feel clean for long periods and avoid sexual attention. I got a few "molecular fragrances" for that purpose but they were either too light (Molecule 01 and Not a Perfume) or too heavy (Après l’Amour). The only one that works for me is Another 13. Another 13 is a citric musk heavy on cetalox. I catalogue Ambroxan and Cetalox as heavy, leaning masculine notes.  I must admit that I prefer the scent of Molecule 01 for myself (a bit more sweet and innocent) but It didn't perform how I wanted it. A man wearing Another 13 is a clean, practical, sexy man (to me). That impression translated into a woman would be something like: too masculine to be sexy, but clean and focused on her own thing today. Yes, I don't think this fragrance is very inviting (on women). I get the same impression with MFK 724. I don't wear Another 13 to indulge myself or others, it has a practical purpose and it does the job!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2163204"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2163204#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2161349" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1693927">stpfau</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-19">05/19/24 16:43</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I really want to love this, since it includes many of my favorite notes, and it’s the kind of minimalist, musky skin scent I’m drawn to.<br />
<br />
But something about it smells stale to me—like a well-loved wool sweater you’ve hand-washed with nice detergent and left to air-dry in a windowless basement. The pear and apple and jasmine notes add some good balance, but they smell a little too ripe and earthy to open up the slightly musty funk that dominates this fragrance.<br />
<br />
It’s not unpleasant, though I wouldn’t call it light or refreshing or exciting. But maybe I just got a bad batch, or maybe it just doesn’t work well on my skin.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2161349"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2161349#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2160997" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2146047" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Scratch &amp; Sniff"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1878218"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1878218.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Scratch &amp; Sniff" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2146047ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2146047" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1878218">Scratch &amp; Sniff</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-04">05/04/24 22:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I initially wrote a scathing review of Another 13.  While I won’t take back anything that I said, because I’m as stubborn as this fragrance itself, I will say that it’s worth a different critique…now that I can actually smell it, at last.<br />
<br />
For weeks of revisiting my sample, I couldn’t smell Another 13.  Like countless others have said, it smelled like nothing.  Perhaps I’m mostly anosmic to Iso E Super.  But then, after repeated exposures and attempts, I finally detected what Another 13 smells like.<br />
<br />
And it was beautiful.  This is the lightest, most airy, most ethereal and most comforting, coziest musk.  The archetypal skin scent.  Another 13 is the thesis of “your skin but better,” and it’s a potion of intimacies, subtleties, attractions and pheromones bottled together.  It’s light as a feather.<br />
<br />
Another 13 is like the ghost or supernatural entity of some scary movie: invisible to many, but, once you finally see it, then you can’t unsee (or, in this case, un-smell) it.<br />
<br />
And yet, like that ghost, it haunts you.  Another 13 is not ever-present.  It’s always there, lingering somewhere in the background, but only deciding in which precise moments it chooses to make itself known.  And then, only when it deigns to, Another 13 declares itself with a haunting refrain.  This fragrance plays, or rather cheats at, an unfair game of hide-and-seek, because it’s sometimes impossible to detect.<br />
<br />
I have a love-hate relationship with Another 13.  It's a dichotomy in a bottle.  When it’s present and detectable, then it's phenomenal and intoxicating.  But when it’s not, it’s infuriating and frustrating.  It has an overhyped but still addictive quality, and I kind of hate myself for buying into that.  Good luck smelling it and then, once you do, good luck forgetting it.<br />
<br />
Another 13 leaves you chasing it: the perfume equivalent of an emotionally unavailable boyfriend.<br />
<br />
I don’t know whether I’ll purchase a bottle, because $230+ seems comically expensive for a fragrance that spends half its time in hiding, and which I’d probably need to douse myself in to get a solid whiff of.  But I’ve proven myself multiple times over to be Le Labo’s bitch (I’m lookin' at you, Santal 33, Vanille 44, Iris 39, and even Baie 19), so this bottle isn’t entirely off the table.<br />
<br />
In five words or less: A ghost of a fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2146047"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2146047#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2145886" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Its woody freshness and musky allure make it my perfect daytime fragrance. Though I may become anosmic to its presence at times, catching a fleeting whiff reignites my passion for it. The numerous compliments I've received over the years validate its allure, solidifying its status as my everyday work perfume. As the seasons shift, I find myself instinctively reaching for Another 13 during the rejuvenating days of spring and the crisp beginnings of fall.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2048848">camrynkm</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-24">04/24/24 23:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I know everyone says iso e smells like woods to them but to me, it evokes something creamy, almost animalic and sweat-like. My best friend says it reminds her of hugging a gay guy at the club who you wont pursue because you’re a girl and he’s a gay guy, but he smells so sexy that it almost convinces you to try anyway. This toes the line between very clean and somewhat.. skanky. If it was any more powerfully musky it would be nauseating- but luckily it’s just plain addictive, and my favorite scent I have ever smelled to this day (save for maybe its excellent summertime sister from floral street, Arizona bloom). Smells sophisticated while still laid back, papery, musky, edged with a sneaky raunchiness. The fruit notes listed don’t translate at all to me, and are completely drowned out by the seemingly bizarre but totally genius cacophony of mysterious synthetics. Completely unisex as it bears absolutely no resemblance to any pre-existing “male” or “female” fragrance- no gourmand accords, headachey florals, spices, or leather to be found. So well blended and harmonious that it comes off as simple, but in actuality is totally complex. Versatile, strange, easy, perfect.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2135583"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2135583#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2134625" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
From me personally, I don't see the dna of BR540 (not even remotely close) but all good-tomato, tomatoe...<br />
I can also tell immediately, based on comments and without even looking at your scent catalogue, that AVxNTvS would be in your repertoire. But I digress...<br />
<br />
One of the many key attributes to the creation of a scent is to not only move you but also to transport you to another (no pun intended) time and place. This scent takes me to the early 2000s (2006-2010) when Tower Records was still the mainstay for all creatives and music aficionados, coffee was still 'cheap' and the idea of being 'social' came in the form of 143 6877 1773...  Anyways, amongst my pretty eclectic collection of frags, this one, I can always come back to without fail and wear with confidence and comfort. A sensual ambroxyde experience indeed...and yes, I am male who loves sports and most frags alike... #believethehype lol<br />
<br />
And lastly...for those that mention that this scent reminds them of high gloss magazines/paper...well, this fragrance was the collaboration of Le Labo and the magazine, Another (still in existence).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />
VERDICT: Smells like a credit card that has been set on fire. Literally and figuratively</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="2025326"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=2025326#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1340656" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1340656" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="KladfvbungMicshk"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/367345"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.367345.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="KladfvbungMicshk" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/L-Artisan-Parfumeur/Passage-d-Enfer-4572.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.4572.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Passage d'Enfer"title="Passage d'Enfer"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1340656ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1340656" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/367345">KladfvbungMicshk</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-05-09">05/09/21 20:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>There’s something very uncanny-valley like about this. It’s good quality in the sense that it’s well-composed, but it’s trying to mimic a musk scent that is just so synthetic it’s creepy. If there was an apocalypse and all that was left were robots and androids, I’m sure they’d be wearing Another 13.<br />
<br />
D&amp;G Light Blue is somewhat similar, but for some reason much more human. Maybe because it includes notes more readily found in nature?<br />
<br />
Anyways, I liked it at first, I could almost convince myself it was cozy. But the more I get to know it the less I like it, and it’s really hard to get off. <br />
<br />
⭐️ for longevity + the fascinating way it slips in and out of detection</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="1340656"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=1340656#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1258891" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1258891" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="bourcet"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1090870"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1090870.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="bourcet" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Kayali-Fragrances/Vanilla-Candy-Rock-Sugar-42-92258.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.92258.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Vanilla Candy Rock Sugar | 42"title="Vanilla Candy Rock Sugar | 42"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1258891ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1258891" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1090870">bourcet</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-12-09">12/09/20 14:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Why is it that I cannot experience the same positivity with this fragrance that others seemingly can? Like, I really want to like this scent! But I cannot. Someone PLEASE explain to me why that is. <br />
<br />
This smells like the Long Island Rail Road 3:01 AM “drunk train.” Greasy pizza, cigarette stench, skunked Heineken, Drakkar Noir. It’s like when your baby spits up in your hair but you’re too tired to do anything about it so you keep getting wafts of powdery Pampers and baby vomit throughout the day. Or for the younger ones in the house tonight: when you “boot and rally” on Frat Row and a little bit of puke gets on the collar of your shirt so you get wafts of bile, Polo Sport and Jäger for the rest of the night. They should rename this Bile 13. <br />
<br />
I remember hating this fragrance when I first tried it years ago. I was pretty new to fragrance then and my nose has since matured, so I figured I’d give it another try in the Nordstrom discovery set. Well, nope. Still hate it. I guess I just really hate that coconut note, if you can even call it that. Is that amyl salicylate? I can get a vibe of unripe banana from it but that note in concert with the woodsiness of the Iso Super E does not make any sense to my nose or to my body chemistry at all. I’m actually a fan of ambrox. Is this creamy, sweet nastiness ambergris? I tend to like frags which feature Iso Super E so I need help understanding this fuckery. <br />
<br />
Molly Sims listed this as one of her “things she cannot live without” on The Cut. What is her skin pH that this smells amazing on her? To me it smells like rotting garbage. She says she gets compliments all the time! What’s that like?? So jealous!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="1258891"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=1258891#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1172120" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1172120" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="archiephillips"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1235761"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1235761.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="archiephillips" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1172120ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1172120" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1235761">archiephillips</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-05-06">05/06/20 04:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Smells almost exactly like Molecule 01 + Molecule 02 + musks.<br />
<br />
It's transparent woods and metallic ambroxan all wrapped up in a musk which begins slightly fruity, but dries down simply. <br />
Once again, the Le Labo pricing knocks this out of contention. I'm not one to complain about prices in reviews, I'm more concerned about if it smells good, but there comes a point when I would never even consider purchasing this because it costs so damn much for what it is. It puts me in the position of choosing between 100ml of Molecule 01 and 100ml of Molecule 02; or 50ml of Another 13. Is Another 13 good enough to justify the difference? Nowhere near.<br />
This might be a good option if you have some kind of vendetta against Escentric Molecules. <br />
<br />
Indifferent.<br />
<br />
(dislike/indifferent/like, but not BW/like a lot, potentially BW/love, definitely BW/masterpiece)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="10131"comment_id="1172120"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Le-Labo/Another-13-10131.html?ccid=1172120#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="10131" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
